(the &#8220;Company&#8221;) issued a press release calling for redemption the entire $1,000,000,000 aggregate principal amount of its outstanding 0.625% Notes due 2022 (CUSIP No.&#160;609207 AV7 / ISIN No.&#160;US609207AV77) (the &#8220;Notes&#8221;), which were issued pursuant to the Indenture, dated as of March&#160;6, 2015 (as supplemented and amended from time to time, the &#8220;Base Indenture&#8221;), by and between the Company and Deutsche Bank Trust Company Americas, as trustee, as supplemented by the Officers&#8217; Certificate of the Company, dated as of July&#160;2, 2020, issued pursuant to Section&#160;301 of the 2015 Base Indenture. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Notes will be redeemed on March&#160;18, 2022 (the &#8220;Redemption Date&#8221;), at a redemption price equal to the greater of (1) 100% of the principal amount of the Notes to be redeemed or (2)&#160;the sum of the present values of each remaining scheduled payment of principal and interest thereon (exclusive of interest accrued to the date of redemption) discounted to the Redemption Date on a semi-annual basis (assuming a <span style="white-space:nowrap">360-day</span> year consisting of twelve <span style="white-space:nowrap">30-day</span> months) at the Treasury Rate (as defined in the Notes) plus 10 basis points, plus accrued and unpaid interest, if any, thereon to, but excluding, the Redemption Date. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company expects to publish the actual redemption price for the Notes in the investor section of its website (http://www.mondelezinternational.com/investors) once it has been determined. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">A copy of the press release is filed as Exhibit 99.2 to this Current Report on Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">8-K.</span> </p> <p style="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Mondel&#275;z International Announces Cash Tender Offer </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">CHICAGO, IL, March&nbsp;3, 2022 &#150; Mondel&#275;z International, Inc. (Nasdaq: MDLZ) (&#147;Mondel&#275;z International&#148;) today
announced its offer to purchase (the&nbsp;&#147;Tender Offer&#148;) for cash up to an aggregate consideration amount, including premium, but excluding any Accrued Interest (as defined below), of $850,000,000 (such amount as it may be amended, the
&#147;Maximum Tender Amount&#148;) of the debt securities listed in the table (the &#147;Notes&#148;), each issued under the applicable indenture, as supplemented by the applicable officers&#146; certificate, governing each series of Notes. </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Details of the Tender Offer </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The consideration paid in the Tender Offer will be determined in the manner described in the Offer to Purchase by reference to the applicable
fixed spread over the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">bid-side</FONT> or <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mid-market</FONT> (as applicable) yield to maturity of the applicable Reference Security (such sum being annualized in the case of the
Sterling Notes) as specified in the table above as calculated by the Dealer Managers for the Tender Offer at 10:00&nbsp;a.m., New York City time, on Thursday, March 17, 2022 (such time and date, as the same may be extended, the &#147;Price
Determination Date&#148;). Holders who validly tender (and who do not validly withdraw) their Notes at or prior to 5:00 p.m., New York City time, on Wednesday, March 16, 2022 (such date and time, as the same may be extended, the &#147;Early Tender
Date&#148;) and whose Notes are accepted for purchase will receive the applicable &#147;Total Consideration,&#148; which includes an early tender premium for the applicable series of Notes set forth in the table above (the &#147;Early Tender
Premium&#148;). Holders who validly tender (and who do not validly withdraw) their Notes after the Early Tender Date and at or prior to 11:59 p.m., New York City time, on Wednesday, March 30, 2022, unless extended (such date and time, as the same
may be extended, the &#147;Expiration Date&#148;), and whose Notes are accepted for purchase will only receive the applicable Tender Consideration per $1,000 or &pound;1,000 principal amount of Notes tendered by such Holders that are accepted for
purchase, which is equal to the applicable Total Consideration minus the Early Tender Premium. In addition to the Total Consideration or the Tender Offer Consideration, as applicable, all Holders of Notes accepted for purchase will also receive
accrued and unpaid interest on such $1,000 or &pound;1,000 principal amount of Notes from the last applicable interest payment date up to, but not including, the applicable settlement date, payable on the applicable settlement date (&#147;Accrued
Interest&#148;). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Assuming the Tender Offer is not extended and the conditions to the Tender Offer are satisfied or waived, Mondel&#275;z
International expects (i)&nbsp;that settlement for Notes validly tendered and not validly withdrawn at or prior to the Early Tender Date and accepted for purchase pursuant to the Tender Offer will be on Friday, March 18, 2022, but Mondel&#275;z
International reserves the right, in its sole discretion, to designate such settlement date at any date following the Early Tender Date, and (ii)&nbsp;that settlement for any Notes validly tendered and not validly withdrawn after the Early Tender
Date and at or prior to the Expiration Date and accepted for purchase will be on Friday, April 1, 2022. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Notes tendered in the Tender
Offer may be validly withdrawn at any time at or prior to 5:00 p.m., New York City time, on Wednesday, March 16, 2022 (such date and time, as the same may be extended, the &#147;Withdrawal Deadline&#148;), but not thereafter unless Mondel&#275;z
International is otherwise required by applicable law to permit withdrawal. </P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The amount of a series of Notes that is purchased in the Tender Offer will be based on the
applicable Acceptance Priority Level for such series as set forth in the table on the front cover of the Offer to Purchase, with &#147;1&#148; being the highest Acceptance Priority Level and &#147;11&#148; being the lowest Acceptance Priority Level,
subject to the 2030&nbsp;Notes SubCap (provided that Notes validly tendered and not validly withdrawn at or prior to the Early Tender Date will be purchased prior to any Notes tendered after the Early Tender Date, regardless of the Acceptance
Priority Level of such Notes validly tendered after the Early Tender Date). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Notwithstanding any other provision of the Tender Offer, the
obligation of Mondel&#275;z International to accept for purchase, and to pay for, any Notes validly tendered and not validly withdrawn is further subject to, and conditioned upon, the successful completion (in Mondel&#275;z International&#146;s sole
opinion) of some form of debt financing designated to raise sufficient funds to purchase all Notes validly tendered and not validly withdrawn, including premium but excluding any Accrued Interest, subject to the Maximum Tender Amount and, in the
case of the 2030 Notes, the 2030 Notes SubCap, and accepted for purchase by Mondel&#275;z International and to pay all fees and expenses in connection with the Tender Offer (the &#147;Financing Condition&#148;), unless Mondel&#275;z International
(in its sole discretion) elects to waive the Financing Condition. The terms of such debt financing will be determined by market conditions and other factors at the time it occurs. No assurances can be given that Mondel&#275;z International will in
fact complete such debt financing. Consummation of the Tender Offer is expressly contingent upon, among other things, Mondel&#275;z International obtaining financing on terms satisfactory to Mondel&#275;z International. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Validly tendered Notes may be withdrawn at any time at or prior to the Withdrawal Deadline. After such time, Holders may not withdraw their
Notes, unless Mondel&#275;z International is otherwise required by applicable law to permit withdrawal, in which case withdrawal rights will be extended, in accordance with applicable law, as Mondel&#275;z International determines to be appropriate
to allow tendering Holders a reasonable opportunity to respond. In the event of a termination of the Tender Offer either in whole or with respect to any series of Notes, any Notes as to which the Tender Offer has been terminated that have been
validly tendered will be promptly returned in accordance with applicable law. Notes tendered pursuant to the Tender Offer and not purchased due to the Maximum Tender Amount, the 2030 Notes SubCap, priority acceptance procedures, proration or a
defect in the tender will be returned to the tendering Holders promptly following the Expiration Date. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Subject to applicable law, the
Tender Offer may be terminated or withdrawn in whole or terminated or withdrawn with respect to any or all series of Notes. Mondel&#275;z International reserves the right, subject to applicable law, to: (i)&nbsp;waive any and all conditions to the
Tender Offer, including the Financing Condition with respect to any or all series of Notes; (ii)&nbsp;extend or terminate the Tender Offer with respect to any or all series of Notes; (iii)&nbsp;increase or decrease the Maximum Tender Amount or the
2030 Notes SubCap; or (iv)&nbsp;otherwise amend the Tender Offer with respect to any or all series of Notes, in each case, in their sole discretion without </P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About Mondel&#275;z International </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Mondel&#275;z International, Inc. (Nasdaq: MDLZ) empowers people to snack right in over 150 countries around the world. With 2021 net revenues
of approximately $29&nbsp;billion, MDLZ is leading the future of snacking with iconic global and local brands such as <I>Oreo</I>, <I>belVita</I> and <I>LU</I> biscuits; <I>Cadbury Dairy Milk</I>, <I>Milka</I> and <I>Toblerone</I> chocolate; <I>Sour
Patch Kids</I> candy and <I>Trident</I> gum. Mondel&#275;z International is a proud member of the Standard and Poor&#146;s 500, Nasdaq 100 and Dow Jones Sustainability Index. </P>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Mondel&#275;z International Calls for </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Redemption of 0.625% Notes Due 2022 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">CHICAGO, IL, March&nbsp;3, 2022 &#150; Mondel&#275;z International, Inc. (Nasdaq: MDLZ) (&#147;Mondel&#275;z International&#148; or the
&#147;Company&#148;) today called for redemption the entire $1,000,000,000 aggregate principal amount of its outstanding 0.625% Notes due 2022 (CUSIP&nbsp;No.&nbsp;609207 AV7 / ISIN No. US609207AV77) (the &#147;Notes&#148;), which were issued
pursuant to the Indenture, dated as of March&nbsp;6, 2015 (as supplemented and amended from time to time, the &#147;Base Indenture&#148;), by and between the Company and Deutsche Bank Trust Company Americas, as trustee, as supplemented by the
Officers&#146; Certificate of the Company, dated as of July&nbsp;2, 2020, issued pursuant to Section&nbsp;301 of the Base Indenture. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The
Notes will be redeemed on March&nbsp;18, 2022 (the &#147;Redemption Date&#148;). The Notes will be redeemed at a redemption price equal to the greater of (1) 100% of the principal amount of the Notes to be redeemed or (2)&nbsp;the sum of the present
values of each remaining scheduled payment of principal and interest thereon (exclusive of interest accrued to the date of redemption) discounted to the Redemption Date on a semi-annual basis (assuming a
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">360-day</FONT> year consisting of twelve <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> months) at the Treasury Rate (as defined in the Notes) plus 10 basis points, plus accrued and unpaid interest, if any, thereon
to, but excluding, the Redemption Date. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company expects to publish the actual redemption prices of the Notes in the investor section
of its website <U>(www.mondelezinternational.com/investors)</U> once they have been determined. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">1 </P>
